date: "2018-07-05"

---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

Based on:

<div class="references" markdown="1">
- https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
- https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html
</div>

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="466" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="470" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="478" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="490" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="494" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="499" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="506" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="521" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="529" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#529" class="Function">_</a> <a id="531" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="533" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="537" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="810" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="817" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#817" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="827" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="836" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="902" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="968" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>
  <a id="Universes.Type"></a><a id="1010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1015" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1017" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1018" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1018" class="Bound">ℓ</a> <a id="1020" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1022" href="Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="1027" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1029" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="1031" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="1035" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1036" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="1041" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1018" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="1042" class="Symbol">)</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

<a id="1536" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="⊥"></a><a id="1541" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1541" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1543" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1544" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1546" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1550" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1555" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1544" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1558" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1871" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1929" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1945" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1952" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1952" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1954" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1956" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1108" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1962" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1970" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1982" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1985" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1985" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1990" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1992" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1982" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1995" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1999" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="2012" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1952" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="2014" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2357" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2364" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2456" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>

  <a id="2444" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2456" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2456" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2462" class="Keyword">field</a>

### Products (×)

### Boolean

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3418" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3423" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3425" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1108" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3433" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3441" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3423" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3452" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3457" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3459" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3423" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3423" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3466" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3466" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3470" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3472" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3423" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3475" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3479" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3495" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3423" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3497" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3614" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3619" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3621" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3622" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3622" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3623" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3625" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3626" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3626" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3628" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3630" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3635" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3622" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3636" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3638" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3640" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3626" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3642" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3644" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3626" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

A more sofisticated composition function that can handle dependent functions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4072" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="4079" class="Number">80</a> <a id="4082" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4086" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a>

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

### Identity Type

Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

<a id="5749" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5620" class="Function">J&#39;</a> <a id="5752" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5753" class="Argument">a</a> <a id="5755" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5757" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5757" class="Bound">a</a><a id="5758" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5760" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5760" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="5762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5762" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="5764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5765" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5241" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="5770" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5757" class="Bound">a</a><a id="5771" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5773" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5775" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5762" class="Bound">d</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6357" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6357" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6366" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6368" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6370" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6371" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6374" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6376" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6378" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6379" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6379" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6381" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6371" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6390" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6392" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6393" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6395" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6379" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6399" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6401" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6406" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6374" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6408" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7229" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7236" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7236" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7256" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7257" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7257" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7259" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7261" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7262" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7262" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7266" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7271" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7257" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7273" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7275" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7284" class="Comment">-- Common combinators for equational reasoning. They allow us to</a>
  <a id="7351" class="Comment">-- write proof in an equational style. These versions have been</a>
  <a id="7417" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

  <a id="7478" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="7485" class="Number">2</a> <a id="7487" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7496" class="Function Operator">_==⟨⟩_</a>

<a id="7781" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7786" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7236" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8085" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8089" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8091" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8093" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8093" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8094" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8096" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8097" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8097" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8099" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8101" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8093" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8107" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8110" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8111" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8113" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8115" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8097" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8118" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8111" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8113" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8133" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8135" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8113" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8137" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8140" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8111" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8142" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8146" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8147" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5241" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8152" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8152" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8153" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8155" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8157" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5241" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8162" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8152" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

#### Associativity of composition

Properties of function composition.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8494" class="Comment">-- Left associativity</a>

<a id="9866" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9871" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8971" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

  <a id="10061" class="Comment">-- Transport</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14726" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14733" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14733" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14742" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14743" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14743" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14746" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14746" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14748" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14750" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14751" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14751" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14753" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14755" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14760" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14743" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14762" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14764" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14765" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14765" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14767" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14769" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14751" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14771" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14778" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14746" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14780" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14782" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14790" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14868" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14908" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14908" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14917" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14919" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14920" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14922" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14922" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14924" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14926" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14928" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14932" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14751" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14933" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14935" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14765" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14939" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14928" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14940" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14943" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14950" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14951" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14743" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14954" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14956" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14746" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14958" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14962" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14908" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14971" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14973" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14973" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14975" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14977" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14978" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14978" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14751" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14983" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14985" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14987" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14971" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14989" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14978" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14991" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14994" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14973" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14996" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14978" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="15001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15001" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="15005" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15007" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15008" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15008" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15010" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15010" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15012" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15014" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15016" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15018" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15020" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14751" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15021" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15023" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14765" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15027" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15016" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15028" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15031" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15033" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15038" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15039" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14743" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15042" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15044" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14746" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15046" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15050" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15052" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15001" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15054" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15054" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15056" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15058" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14908" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15067" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15050" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15054" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="15074" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

A particular case of naturality on the identity function.

## Fibers

Contractible types with a center of contraction.

## Equivalence

    <a id="18355" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18423" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18488" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18505" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18505" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18516" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18519" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18519" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18521" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18523" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18318" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18525" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18527" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18332" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18528" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18530" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18538" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18310" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18541" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18543" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18313" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18545" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18599" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18670" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22022" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="22029" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22029" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22046" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22047" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22047" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22050" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22052" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22054" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22055" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22055" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22057" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22059" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22064" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22047" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22066" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22068" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22069" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22071" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22073" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22050" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22080" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22082" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22091" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22158" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22204" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22204" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22222" <a id="22936" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="22941" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22029" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23207" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23214" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23214" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23232" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23233" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23234" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23236" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23245" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23316" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23354" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23354" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23360" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23362" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23363" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23233" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23373" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23375" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23233" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="23386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23354" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23392" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23392" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23394" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23396" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23397" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23397" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23399" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="23401" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23392" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23404" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23406" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23409" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23397" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23411" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23414" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23399" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23415" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23417" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2929" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="23419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1703" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="23421" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23422" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23397" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23424" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23399" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23428" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23433" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="23498" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>

<a id="23919" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23214" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24154" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24161" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24161" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24174" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24183" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24252" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24267" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24274" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24276" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24278" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24279" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24282" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24283" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24283" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24285" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24287" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24292" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24278" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24293" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24295" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24297" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24278" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24306" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24313" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24313" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24315" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24317" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24319" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24319" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24321" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24323" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24325" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24313" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24326" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24328" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24330" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24319" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24332" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24321" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24336" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24341" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24376" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24376" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24382" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24384" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24386" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24387" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24389" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24396" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24397" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24386" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24403" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24407" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24376" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24413" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24414" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24414" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24415" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24417" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24419" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24421" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24422" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24427" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24414" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24428" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24441" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24507" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24525" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24525" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24532" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24534" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24536" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24536" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24539" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24541" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24543" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24545" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24546" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24546" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24548" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24550" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24555" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24536" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24557" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24559" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24561" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24562" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24564" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24566" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24546" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24568" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24570" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24575" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24539" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24577" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24588" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24590" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24592" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24592" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24594" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24596" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24546" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24597" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24599" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24601" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24608" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24609" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24562" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24592" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24612" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24615" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24617" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24624" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24626" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24626" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24628" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24630" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24546" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24631" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24633" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24635" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24562" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24637" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24626" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24638" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24642" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24525" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24649" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24649" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24655" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24655" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24657" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24657" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24659" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24661" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20352" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24668" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24672" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24674" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24649" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24680" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24682" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24683" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24655" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24685" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24686" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24688" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24689" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24657" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24691" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24670" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24692" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24697" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24755" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24755" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24767" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24769" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24771" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24771" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24774" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24774" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24776" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24778" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24780" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24781" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24781" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24783" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24785" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24790" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24771" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24792" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24794" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24796" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24797" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24797" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24799" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24801" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24774" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24808" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24824" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24826" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24833" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24781" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24835" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24837" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24844" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24797" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24846" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24848" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24855" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24856" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24781" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24858" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2754" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24860" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24797" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24861" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24925" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24930" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24161" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25138" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25145" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25145" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25150" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25159" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25230" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

  <a id="25284" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25246" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25290" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25290" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25292" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="25294" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25295" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25295" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25297" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25297" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="25299" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25301" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25290" class="Bound">A</a><a id="25302" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25304" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25306" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24267" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="25313" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25314" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25295" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="25316" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5194" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="25319" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25297" class="Bound">y</a><a id="25320" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="25845" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25850" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25145" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28113" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27331" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28362" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28369" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28382" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28383" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28386" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28388" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28390" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28391" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28400" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28383" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28402" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28404" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28405" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28409" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28414" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28386" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28416" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28418" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28427" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>

## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31219" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31226" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31226" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31240" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31241" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31241" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31244" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31246" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31248" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31249" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31251" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31258" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31241" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31260" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31262" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31263" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31265" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31267" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31272" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31244" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31274" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31276" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33972" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

     <a id="35436" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2472" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35049" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35363" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35449" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35451" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4086" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2472" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35457" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35363" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7574" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20352" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35474" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35475" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19621" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35491" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35363" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35492" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7574" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35507" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7673" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35508" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35511" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35516" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34257" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35715" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="35722" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35722" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="35733" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="35777" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="UnivalenceAxiom"></a><a id="35784" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35784" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="35800" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35801" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35801" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35802" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35804" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35805" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35805" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35807" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35807" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35809" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35811" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1010" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="35816" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35801" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35817" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35819" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="36519" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="36524" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35784" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="36540" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Somme lemmas about Univelance

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="36618" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36621" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36660" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36721" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36770" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36789" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36804" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36869" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36922" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36940" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36951" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36954" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="37026" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37051" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37147" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37168" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37183" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37290" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37395" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37474" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37550" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37633" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37656" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37667" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37682" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37768" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37797" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37816" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37904" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="38014" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38102" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38145" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38161" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38164" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38198" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38278" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38298" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38313" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38383" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38448" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38497" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38515" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="38529" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
